/*
  Enhanced Soldier Customization for Long War by eclipse666
  
  This mod allows you to change your soldier's head size, body size and voice pitch from the soldier customisation screen.
  The range of available skin colours has also been greatly increased - you're no longer limited to skin tones.
  
  You can create a "sectoid" soldier by selecting a small body size, large head, and setting the voice to high pitched.
  Put a full face helmet on it and you'll find it hard to tell the difference.
  
  Similarly you could create muton and berserker soldiers with large bodies and heads, and deep voices.
  
  SHIV body size, weapon size and armour colour can be customized too! 
  
  Note that SHIV colours will appear duller than they actually are while in the customisation screen due to
  the background lighting. Return to the squad line up to see the SHIV colour as it will actually appear during battle.
  
  If you want new soldiers to have their head sizes, body sizes and voice pitches randomized then please install the
  "Enhanced Randomized Soldiers" mod included with this mod as well. It can also create "alien" soldiers!
  
  Install with PatcherGUI 7.1 or better. This has been tested with Long War beta 15f but it should work with earlier versions too.
  If you've installed a previous version you'll have to uninstall it first before apply this new one or you will get an error. 
  
  If you have trouble with this you can simply reinstall Long War and then install this mod immediately after.
  
  1.0a Initial release
  1.0b Parameter ranges increased to allow for finer control
       Voice Pitch now ranges from 1 to 99 (50 = normal)
	   Head Size now ranges from 1 to 199 (50 = normal, 1=headless)
	   Body Size now ranges from 1 to 99 (50 = normal)
  1.0c Same as 1.0b but this mod now comes bundled with Enhanced Randomized Soldiers. 
  1.0d SHIV Body size can now also be set. Unfortunately custom SHIV colours do not seem to be possible.
       Max head size now 199 (was 119 before)
  1.0e SHIV Weapon size can now be set via "Head Size". 
	   SHIV Armor tint can now be set.
	   Fixed bug that reset body/voice/head size when skin colour changed
       Note that if you have more than 1 SHIV on a mission, they will all be set to the
	   same color as the last SHIV. I don't know why this happens... yet.
  1.0f Each SHIV now correctly displays in it's own colour when more than 1 is selected for a mission
       (previously all SHIVs would take on colour of the first SHIV)
  1.0g SHIV's name now appears on the SHIV health 'flag' (instead of just "SHIV"). Because SHIV's are special.
       SHIV's name is now used in the "SHIV was destroyed" message 
  1.0h "Perfect Information" second wave option now displays "SHIV" correctly in messages
       (would display SHIV~### before, where ### is the encoded SHIV colour and size)
  1.0i Tweaked helmet/hair scaling to minimize 'hair float' issue for soldiers with small to normal head sizes.
       The optional "Enhanced Randomized Soldiers" mods included with this mod now also include "Gender and Race Aware" mod 
	   functionality which allows you to use custom name lists that include race and gender info. 
  1.0j Merged deployment position fix (included in LW 1.0) into the mod.
       Fixed some more instances where SHIV name would display encoded colour and size info
  	  
*/
